Alcohol is considered a crucial element in creating the fragrance variations in synthetic perfumes, with alcohol making up as much as 50% to 70% of a perfume bottle. In contrast, perfume essential oils contain very little or even no alcohol. Instead, oils like Jojoba or grapeseed oil are often used to create various scents in essential oils.
